        <div id="readme" class="Box-body readme blob js-code-block-container p-5 p-xl-6 gist-border-0">
    <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-awesome-mac" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#awesome-mac"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Awesome Mac</h1>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/sindresorhus/awesome"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/b468692d179cad746d6d5ea4ac3e143820f67b56a31c4da6ed97500a2976ec61/68747470733a2f2f6a617977636a6c6f76652e6769746875622e696f2f73622f69636f2f617765736f6d652e737667" src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/c91e0bbd93918d34afce3fb7888756219357c45de1c527fe0ebec0ffa481d487/68747470733a2f2f6a617977636a6c6f76652e6769746875622e696f2f73622f6c616e672f656e676c6973682e737667" href="https://gitter.im/awesome-mac/en?utm_source=badge&amp;utm_medium=badge&amp;utm_campaign=pr-badge&amp;utm_content=body_badge" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/7fd8a66a20990a38623faa65e0b1cf94f13f9ff4d69409597f43aaf983852c7b/68747470733a2f2f6a617977636a6c6f76652e6769746875622e696f2f73622f69636f2f7365676d656e746661756c742e737667" src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/9a073523c4b70663d0d96b76019cffe76906adaaa67908551c0fcf11e763dec6/68747470733a2f2f6a617977636a6c6f76652e6769746875622e696f2f73622f69636f2f776569626f2e737667" alt="" data-canonical-src="https://jaywcjlove.github.io/sb/ico/weibo.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> <a href="#backers"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/e1994da3a9456f3532e934134c77cf1fb87f1e63371cb68e375b4bc9a8caf76c/68747470733a2f2f6f70656e636f6c6c6563746976652e636f6d2f617765736f6d652d6d61632f6261636b6572732f62616467652e737667" src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/eb19d6c680c1188febdc03e613b03748c65d3f00f682e9a851586b3691705d00/68747470733a2f2f6f70656e636f6c6c6563746976652e636f6d2f617765736f6d652d6d61632f73706f6e736f72732f62616467652e737667" alt="Sponsors on Open Collective" data-canonical-src="https://opencollective.com/awesome-mac/sponsors/badge.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>

<p dir="auto"> 现在我们变得非常大，与最初的想法不同，如今我们需要收集各种类别非常好用的 Mac 应用程序、软件以及工具。通过 Pull Request 或者 <a href="https://github.com/jaywcjlove/awesome-mac/issues/new/choose">issues</a> 给我推荐优秀好用的Mac应用，很显然我是一个资深 Mac 用户，我需要它们帮助我快乐、高效的工作，同时也分享给你。文档格式参照 <a href="https://github.com/sindresorhus/awesome">awesome</a>。</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>说明</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="/jaywcjlove/awesome-mac/blob/master/README.md">English</a> | <a href="/jaywcjlove/awesome-mac/blob/master/README-zh.md">中文</a></p>

<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/b4f0d5b4dc3b3a13e565abae2db246dd57e677622035c3a84fe46eb20425c6eb/68747470733a2f2f6a617977636a6c6f76652e6769746875622e696f2f73622f69636f2f6d696e2d667265652e737667"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/b4f0d5b4dc3b3a13e565abae2db246dd57e677622035c3a84fe46eb20425c6eb/68747470733a2f2f6a617977636a6c6f76652e6769746875622e696f2f73622f69636f2f6d696e2d667265652e737667" alt="Freeware" title="免费软件" data-canonical-src="https://jaywcjlove.github.io/sb/ico/min-free.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> 表示 <strong>免费</strong> 使用，或者个人 <strong>免费</strong> ；<br>

<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/491b767d4b8fe216d87d95e28b52a53d86683974780fb6110b0cc225edf6e2d8/68747470733a2f2f6a617977636a6c6f76652e6769746875622e696f2f73622f69636f2f6d696e2d617765736f6d652e737667"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/491b767d4b8fe216d87d95e28b52a53d86683974780fb6110b0cc225edf6e2d8/68747470733a2f2f6a617977636a6c6f76652e6769746875622e696f2f73622f69636f2f6d696e2d617765736f6d652e737667" alt="Awesome List" title="Awesome List" data-canonical-src="https://jaywcjlove.github.io/sb/ico/min-awesome.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> 表示项目的相应 <strong>Awesome list</strong> 的超链接；</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-目录" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#目录"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>目录</h2>

<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-设计工具" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#设计工具"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>设计工具</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://secure.flyingmeat.com/acorn/" rel="nofollow">Acorn</a> - 一个像 PS，全面的功能集的图像编辑器。</li>
<li><a href="https://affinity.serif.com/en-us/designer/" rel="nofollow">Affinity Designer</a> - 矢量图像设计工具，可以是 Adobe Illustrator 的替代。</li>
<li><a href="https://affinity.serif.com/en-us/photo/" rel="nofollow">Affinity Photo</a> - 光栅图像设计工具，可以替代 Adobe PS 图象处理软件。</li>
<li><a href="http://al.chemy.org/" rel="nofollow">Alchemy</a> - 开源的绘图工具软件，用于素描、会话以及一种新的绘图方式。<a href="http://svn.al.chemy.org/" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/3481414765df8f5f81444651c05cdf78325f0ede49471c53d29dffd443090eba/68747470733a2f2f6a617977636a6c6f76652e6769746875622e696f2f73622f69636f2f6d696e2d6f73732e737667" alt="Open-Source Software" title="开源软件" data-canonical-src="https://jaywcjlove.github.io/sb/ico/min-oss.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></li>

<p dir="auto"><em>使用 <a href="https://github.com/phinze/homebrew-cask">Homebrew Cask</a> 将通过命令安装即为简单。开发人员使用的<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Quick_Look" rel="nofollow">Quick Look</a>插件列表。如果手动安装，你可将下载的 <code>.qlgenerator</code> 文件移动到 <code>~/Library/QuickLook</code> 运行 <code>qlmanage -r</code></em></p>

</ul>

<ul dir="auto">
